# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes`, `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`, `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api`, `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd`

# Kubernetes Admission Webhook Processing Chain

## Your Task

Trace the admission webhook processing chain in Kubernetes. Find Go source files across kubernetes/kubernetes and kubernetes/api that implement: the generic Webhook dispatcher (in pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/), the mutating webhook dispatcher with reinvocation logic, the validating webhook dispatcher with parallel dispatch, the WebhookAccessor abstraction layer, and the MutatingWebhookConfiguration/ValidatingWebhookConfiguration API type definitions.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [

  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

### Key Components Found:

1. **Generic Webhook Framework** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/`)
   - Core `Dispatcher` interface for webhook dispatch
   - `Webhook` struct orchestrating the admission flow
   - `ShouldCallHook()` method determining webhook eligibility

2. **WebhookAccessor Abstraction** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`)

   - `mutatingWebhookAccessor` and `validatingWebhookAccessor` implementations
   - Lazy initialization of REST clients and selectors

3. **Mutating Webhook Dispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`)
   - Sophisticated reinvocation logic via `webhookReinvokeContext`
   - Tracks `NeverReinvocationPolicy` vs `IfNeededReinvocationPolicy`
   - Sequential webhook execution with object patching
   - Detects changes to trigger reinvocation of eligible webhooks

4. **Validating Webhook Dispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`)
   - **Parallel dispatch** using goroutines and `sync.WaitGroup`
   - Pre-compiles versioned attributes for efficiency
   - Panic recovery to isolate webhook failures
   - Error collection through buffered channel (capacity = 2x webhooks)

\"Dispatch\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes admission webhook processing chain is structured as a hierarchical dispatcher architecture with two parallel pipelines for mutating and validating webhooks.\\n\\n## Architecture Overview\\n\\n### 1. Generic Webhook Framework (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/)\\n\\nThe `generic` package provides the foundational abstraction layer for webhook processing:\\n\\n- **interfaces.go**: Defines core abstractions:\\n  - `Dispatcher` interface: The main contract for webhook dispatch with method `Dispatch(ctx context.Context, a admission.Attributes, o admission.ObjectInterfaces, hooks []webhook.WebhookAccessor) error`\\n  - `Source` interface: Abstracts webhook configuration source, providing `Webhooks() []webhook.WebhookAccessor`\\n  - `VersionedAttributeAccessor` interface: Handles versioning of admission attributes for different GVKs\\n  - `WebhookInvocation` struct: Encapsulates invocation details (Webhook, Resource, Subresource, Kind)\\n\\n- **webhook.go**: Implements the generic `Webhook` struct that orchestrates the admission flow:\\n  - `NewWebhook()`: Factory function that creates a Webhook with a source factory and dispatcher factory\\n  - `Dispatch()` method: Entry point that retrieves webhooks from the source and delegates to the dispatcher\\n  - `ShouldCallHook()` method: Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selector, object selector, rules matching, and CEL match conditions\\n\\n### 2. WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer (webhook/accessors.go)\\n\\nThe `WebhookAccessor` interface provides a unified abstraction over both mutating and validating webhooks (which have slightly different fields):\\n\\n- Implements methods to access webhook metadata: GetName(), GetUID(), GetRules(), GetFailurePolicy(), GetTimeoutSeconds(), GetClientConfig(), etc.\\n- Two concrete implementations:\\n  - `mutatingWebhookAccessor`: Wraps `v1.MutatingWebhook` with UID and configuration name\\n  - `validatingWebhookAccessor`: Wraps `v1.ValidatingWebhook` with UID and configuration name\\n- Uses sync.Once for lazy initialization of selectors and REST clients\\n\\n### 3. Configuration Management Layer\\n\\nTwo configuration managers manage webhook configuration objects and create webhook accessors:\\n\\n- **mutating_webhook_manager.go**: \\n  - `mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source`\\n  - `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager()`: Creates manager from SharedInformerFactory\\n  - Caches webhook accessors by configuration name for efficiency\\n  - `Webhooks()` method returns sorted list of `WebhookAccessor` objects\\n\\n- **validating_webhook_manager.go**:\\n  - `validatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source`\\n  - `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager()`: Creates manager from SharedInformerFactory\\n  - Similar caching and sorting strategy as mutating manager\\n  - Maintains informer event handlers for dynamic updates\\n\\n### 4. Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic\\n\\nThe mutating webhook pipeline (**webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**) implements sophisticated reinvocation logic:\\n\\n- **mutatingDispatcher struct**: Implements `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- **Dispatch() method**: \\n  - Retrieves or initializes `webhookReinvokeContext` from the reinvocation context\\n  - Tracks which webhooks have been previously invoked using reinvocation policy\\n  - For each webhook, calls `ShouldCallHook()` to determine if it matches\\n  - Checks if object has changed (from other admission plugins) to trigger reinvocation\\n  - Skips webhooks with `NeverReinvocationPolicy` during reinvocation\\n  - Calls `callAttrMutatingHook()` which patches the object\\n  - Records patches in audit annotations with `PatchAuditAnnotationPrefix`\\n  - If webhook patches the object, sets `ShouldReinvoke()` flag to reinvoke earlier eligible plugins\\n  - Webhooks with `IfNeededReinvocationPolicy` are registered for potential reinvocation\\n\\n- **webhookReinvokeContext**: Tracks invocation state across reinvocation rounds:\\n  - `ShouldReinvokeWebhook(uid)`: Checks if webhook should be called in reinvocation\\n  - `RequireReinvokingPreviouslyInvokedPlugins()`: Marks that reinvocation is needed\\n  - `AddReinvocableWebhookToPreviouslyInvoked()`: Records webhooks that support reinvocation\\n\\n### 5. Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch\\n\\nThe validating webhook pipeline (**webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**) implements parallel execution:\\n\\n- **validatingDispatcher struct**: Implements `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- **Dispatch() method**:\\n  - First collects all relevant hooks by calling `ShouldCallHook()` for each webhook\\n  - Pre-compiles versioned attributes for all required GVKs to avoid redundant conversions\\n  - **Parallel execution**: Uses `sync.WaitGroup` and goroutines to call hooks concurrently\\n  - Each goroutine calls `callHook()` with its own invocation and versioned attribute\\n  - Collects errors in an error channel with capacity for panic recovery (2x hooks)\\n  - Implements panic recovery with `utilruntime.HandleCrash()` to prevent one webhook panic from crashing the API server\\n  - Handles failure policies (Ignore vs Fail) for each webhook independently\\n  - Records metrics for each webhook (success, latency, rejection reason)\\n  - Returns first error encountered, or nil if all validations pass\\n\\n### 6. Plugin Layer\\n\\nTwo plugin implementations bridge the admission system with the webhook framework:\\n\\n- **mutating/plugin.go**:\\n  - `Plugin` wraps `generic.Webhook`\\n  - Implements `admission.MutationInterface`\\n  - `NewMutatingWebhook()`: Creates plugin with `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager` as source\\n  - Uses `newMutatingDispatcher()` factory for the mutating dispatcher\\n  - `Admit()` method calls `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n- **validating/plugin.go**:\\n  - `Plugin` wraps `generic.Webhook`\\n  - Implements `admission.ValidationInterface`\\n  - `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()`: Creates plugin with `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager` as source\\n  - Uses `newValidatingDispatcher()` factory for the validating dispatcher\\n  - `Validate()` method calls `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n### 7. API Type Definitions\\n\\nThe API layer defines the webhook configuration resources:\\n\\n- **admissionregistration/v1/types.go** (current stable version):\\n  - `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` struct: Cluster-scoped resource containing list of `MutatingWebhook` objects\\n  - `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` struct: Cluster-scoped resource containing list of `ValidatingWebhook` objects\\n  - `MutatingWebhook` fields: Name, ClientConfig, Rules, FailurePolicy, MatchPolicy, NamespaceSelector, ObjectSelector, SideEffects, TimeoutSeconds, AdmissionReviewVersions, ReinvocationPolicy, MatchConditions\\n  - `ValidatingWebhook` fields: Same as MutatingWebhook\\n  - `ReinvocationPolicyType`: Enum with \\\"Never\\\" and \\\"IfNeeded\\\" values (only in MutatingWebhook)\\n\\n- **admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go** (deprecated in v1.16, removed in v1.22):\\n  - Same structure as v1 but marked as deprecated\\n  - `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` and `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` with identical fields\\n\\n## Processing Chain Flow\\n\\n1. **Admission Request**: API server invokes `Plugin.Admit()` (mutating) or `Plugin.Validate()` (validating)\\n2. **Generic Dispatch**: Calls `Webhook.Dispatch()` in generic/webhook.go\\n3. **Configuration Retrieval**: Gets webhooks from manager's `Source.Webhooks()` which lists current configurations\\n4. **Concrete Dispatcher**: Calls `dispatcher.Dispatch()` with webhook accessors\\n5. **Mutating Path**: \\n   - Handles reinvocation context\\n   - Iterates webhooks sequentially\\n   - Patches object for each webhook\\n   - Tracks changes to trigger reinvocation\\n6. **Validating Path**:\\n   - Pre-processes all webhooks\\n   - Spawns parallel goroutines for concurrent validation\\n   - Collects results with error channel\\n7. **Response**: Returns nil on success or aggregated error\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Strategy Pattern**: `Dispatcher` interface allows different dispatch strategies (mutating vs validating)\\n- **Adapter Pattern**: `WebhookAccessor` unifies v1.MutatingWebhook and v1.ValidatingWebhook APIs\\n- **Observer Pattern**: Configuration managers use informers for dynamic webhook updates\\n- **Factory Pattern**: Dispatcher factories inject concrete dispatcher implementations\\n- **Lazy Evaluation**: Configuration managers use lazy caching to avoid redundant CEL compilation\\n- **Reinvocation Pattern**: Mutating webhooks can request reinvocation if previous plugins modified the object\\n- **Parallel Execution**: Validating webhooks use goroutines for concurrent execution\\n\"\n}\n",

\"Dispatch\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes admission webhook processing chain is structured as a hierarchical dispatcher architecture with two parallel pipelines for mutating and validating webhooks.\\n\\n## Architecture Overview\\n\\n### 1. Generic Webhook Framework (pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/)\\n\\nThe `generic` package provides the foundational abstraction layer for webhook processing:\\n\\n- **interfaces.go**: Defines core abstractions:\\n  - `Dispatcher` interface: The main contract for webhook dispatch with method `Dispatch(ctx context.Context, a admission.Attributes, o admission.ObjectInterfaces, hooks []webhook.WebhookAccessor) error`\\n  - `Source` interface: Abstracts webhook configuration source, providing `Webhooks() []webhook.WebhookAccessor`\\n  - `VersionedAttributeAccessor` interface: Handles versioning of admission attributes for different GVKs\\n  - `WebhookInvocation` struct: Encapsulates invocation details (Webhook, Resource, Subresource, Kind)\\n\\n- **webhook.go**: Implements the generic `Webhook` struct that orchestrates the admission flow:\\n  - `NewWebhook()`: Factory function that creates a Webhook with a source factory and dispatcher factory\\n  - `Dispatch()` method: Entry point that retrieves webhooks from the source and delegates to the dispatcher\\n  - `ShouldCallHook()` method: Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selector, object selector, rules matching, and CEL match conditions\\n\\n### 2. WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer (webhook/accessors.go)\\n\\nThe `WebhookAccessor` interface provides a unified abstraction over both mutating and validating webhooks (which have slightly different fields):\\n\\n- Implements methods to access webhook metadata: GetName(), GetUID(), GetRules(), GetFailurePolicy(), GetTimeoutSeconds(), GetClientConfig(), etc.\\n- Two concrete implementations:\\n  - `mutatingWebhookAccessor`: Wraps `v1.MutatingWebhook` with UID and configuration name\\n  - `validatingWebhookAccessor`: Wraps `v1.ValidatingWebhook` with UID and configuration name\\n- Uses sync.Once for lazy initialization of selectors and REST clients\\n\\n### 3. Configuration Management Layer\\n\\nTwo configuration managers manage webhook configuration objects and create webhook accessors:\\n\\n- **mutating_webhook_manager.go**: \\n  - `mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source`\\n  - `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager()`: Creates manager from SharedInformerFactory\\n  - Caches webhook accessors by configuration name for efficiency\\n  - `Webhooks()` method returns sorted list of `WebhookAccessor` objects\\n\\n- **validating_webhook_manager.go**:\\n  - `validatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source`\\n  - `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager()`: Creates manager from SharedInformerFactory\\n  - Similar caching and sorting strategy as mutating manager\\n  - Maintains informer event handlers for dynamic updates\\n\\n### 4. Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic\\n\\nThe mutating webhook pipeline (**webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**) implements sophisticated reinvocation logic:\\n\\n- **mutatingDispatcher struct**: Implements `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- **Dispatch() method**: \\n  - Retrieves or initializes `webhookReinvokeContext` from the reinvocation context\\n  - Tracks which webhooks have been previously invoked using reinvocation policy\\n  - For each webhook, calls `ShouldCallHook()` to determine if it matches\\n  - Checks if object has changed (from other admission plugins) to trigger reinvocation\\n  - Skips webhooks with `NeverReinvocationPolicy` during reinvocation\\n  - Calls `callAttrMutatingHook()` which patches the object\\n  - Records patches in audit annotations with `PatchAuditAnnotationPrefix`\\n  - If webhook patches the object, sets `ShouldReinvoke()` flag to reinvoke earlier eligible plugins\\n  - Webhooks with `IfNeededReinvocationPolicy` are registered for potential reinvocation\\n\\n- **webhookReinvokeContext**: Tracks invocation state across reinvocation rounds:\\n  - `ShouldReinvokeWebhook(uid)`: Checks if webhook should be called in reinvocation\\n  - `RequireReinvokingPreviouslyInvokedPlugins()`: Marks that reinvocation is needed\\n  - `AddReinvocableWebhookToPreviouslyInvoked()`: Records webhooks that support reinvocation\\n\\n### 5. Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch\\n\\nThe validating webhook pipeline (**webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**) implements parallel execution:\\n\\n- **validatingDispatcher struct**: Implements `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- **Dispatch() method**:\\n  - First collects all relevant hooks by calling `ShouldCallHook()` for each webhook\\n  - Pre-compiles versioned attributes for all required GVKs to avoid redundant conversions\\n  - **Parallel execution**: Uses `sync.WaitGroup` and goroutines to call hooks concurrently\\n  - Each goroutine calls `callHook()` with its own invocation and versioned attribute\\n  - Collects errors in an error channel with capacity for panic recovery (2x hooks)\\n  - Implements panic recovery with `utilruntime.HandleCrash()` to prevent one webhook panic from crashing the API server\\n  - Handles failure policies (Ignore vs Fail) for each webhook independently\\n  - Records metrics for each webhook (success, latency, rejection reason)\\n  - Returns first error encountered, or nil if all validations pass\\n\\n### 6. Plugin Layer\\n\\nTwo plugin implementations bridge the admission system with the webhook framework:\\n\\n- **mutating/plugin.go**:\\n  - `Plugin` wraps `generic.Webhook`\\n  - Implements `admission.MutationInterface`\\n  - `NewMutatingWebhook()`: Creates plugin with `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager` as source\\n  - Uses `newMutatingDispatcher()` factory for the mutating dispatcher\\n  - `Admit()` method calls `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n- **validating/plugin.go**:\\n  - `Plugin` wraps `generic.Webhook`\\n  - Implements `admission.ValidationInterface`\\n  - `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()`: Creates plugin with `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager` as source\\n  - Uses `newValidatingDispatcher()` factory for the validating dispatcher\\n  - `Validate()` method calls `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n### 7. API Type Definitions\\n\\nThe API layer defines the webhook configuration resources:\\n\\n- **admissionregistration/v1/types.go** (current stable version):\\n  - `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` struct: Cluster-scoped resource containing list of `MutatingWebhook` objects\\n  - `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` struct: Cluster-scoped resource containing list of `ValidatingWebhook` objects\\n  - `MutatingWebhook` fields: Name, ClientConfig, Rules, FailurePolicy, MatchPolicy, NamespaceSelector, ObjectSelector, SideEffects, TimeoutSeconds, AdmissionReviewVersions, ReinvocationPolicy, MatchConditions\\n  - `ValidatingWebhook` fields: Same as MutatingWebhook\\n  - `ReinvocationPolicyType`: Enum with \\\"Never\\\" and \\\"IfNeeded\\\" values (only in MutatingWebhook)\\n\\n- **admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go** (deprecated in v1.16, removed in v1.22):\\n  - Same structure as v1 but marked as deprecated\\n  - `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` and `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` with identical fields\\n\\n## Processing Chain Flow\\n\\n1. **Admission Request**: API server invokes `Plugin.Admit()` (mutating) or `Plugin.Validate()` (validating)\\n2. **Generic Dispatch**: Calls `Webhook.Dispatch()` in generic/webhook.go\\n3. **Configuration Retrieval**: Gets webhooks from manager's `Source.Webhooks()` which lists current configurations\\n4. **Concrete Dispatcher**: Calls `dispatcher.Dispatch()` with webhook accessors\\n5. **Mutating Path**: \\n   - Handles reinvocation context\\n   - Iterates webhooks sequentially\\n   - Patches object for each webhook\\n   - Tracks changes to trigger reinvocation\\n6. **Validating Path**:\\n   - Pre-processes all webhooks\\n   - Spawns parallel goroutines for concurrent validation\\n   - Collects results with error channel\\n7. **Response**: Returns nil on success or aggregated error\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Strategy Pattern**: `Dispatcher` interface allows different dispatch strategies (mutating vs validating)\\n- **Adapter Pattern**: `WebhookAccessor` unifies v1.MutatingWebhook and v1.ValidatingWebhook APIs\\n- **Observer Pattern**: Configuration managers use informers for dynamic webhook updates\\n- **Factory Pattern**: Dispatcher factories inject concrete dispatcher implementations\\n- **Lazy Evaluation**: Configuration managers use lazy caching to avoid redundant CEL compilation\\n- **Reinvocation Pattern**: Mutating webhooks can request reinvocation if previous plugins modified the object\\n- **Parallel Execution**: Validating webhooks use goroutines for concurrent execution\\n\"\n}\n",
